data-pb-id="hp-responsive-cube-3-combo" id="fc00Zp1GvDlmFs"> <div class="pb-ad pb-ad-prod ad-300x250 relative"> <div id="label_hp_1615" class="ad-caption-text align-center     (function() {
      let adFlag = true
      //Check optimera smart refresh enabled or not
      if(trb.data.ads.optimera && (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) && (true)) {
        let oInsights = window.oVa.insights ? window.oVa.insights : {}
        let oRemoveAds = oInsights.ilv ? oInsights.ilv : ''
        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_2_/') != -1 && true) {
          let label = document.getElementById('label_hp_1615')
          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false
        }
      }
      if(adFlag) {
        
          //FetchBids for all ads
          if (((!DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true) || (DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true)) && (true && window.apstag) && ((true && window.headertag) || (false && window.PWT))) {
            let params = {
              id: 'hp_1615',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }
            if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !'[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'),
              sizemapDimensions = !''.length ? null : JSON.parse('')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1615'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1615'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }
          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x600/300x250_2_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_300x600/300x250_2_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_2_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_1615',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_300x600/300x250_2_/',
              adType: 'cube',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[300, 600], [300, 250]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()

    (function() {
      let adFlag = true
      //Check optimera smart refresh enabled or not
      if(trb.data.ads.optimera && (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) && (true)) {

        }

          //FetchBids for all ads

              id: 'hp_1608',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }
            if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !'[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'),
              sizemapDimensions = !''.length ? null : JSON.parse('')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1608'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1608'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }
          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_1608',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/',
              adType: 'cube',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[300, 600], [300, 250]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()

              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1507'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1507'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }
          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_1x2_1_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_1x2_1_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_1x2_1_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_1507',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_1x2_1_/',
              adType: '1x2',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.chicagotribune/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[1, 2]]',
              sizemapString: '',
              sizemapRefresh: 'false',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: false,
              includeInIndexExchange: false,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
  </script> </div>
